# ██████╗ ██╗██╗   ██╗███████╗██████╗ ███████╗
# ██╔══██╗██║██║   ██║██╔════╝██╔══██╗██╔════╝
# ██║  ██║██║██║   ██║█████╗  ██████╔╝███████╗
# ██║  ██║██║╚██╗ ██╔╝██╔══╝  ██╔══██╗╚════██║
# ██████╔╝██║ ╚████╔╝ ███████╗██║  ██║███████║
# ╚═════╝ ╚═╝  ╚═══╝  ╚══════╝╚═╝  ╚═╝╚══════╝

#####################################################################################################################################################

#####################################################################################################################################################
#####################################################################################################################################################

infamy_international_trade_pariah = {
	is_shown = {
		infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
	}
}

infamy_international_trade = {
	is_shown = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
	}
}

has_national_stockpile = {
	is_shown = {
		has_building = building_national_stockpile
	}
}

is_national_stockpile = {
	is_shown = {
		is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
	}
}

not_is_national_stockpile = {
	is_shown = {
		not = {
			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		}
	}
}

#grain
trade_grain_budget_panel = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_grain_budget_panel
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_wood_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_coal_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_iron_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_sulfur_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_lead_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_oil_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_dye_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_silk_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_rubber_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

trade_grain_budget_panel_show = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_grain_budget_panel = 1
	}
}

			name = trade_small_arms_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_artillery_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_tanks_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_aeroplanes_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_manowars_budget_panel
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_ironclads_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

trade_manowars_budget_panel_show = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_manowars_budget_panel = 1
	}
}

#ironclads
trade_ironclads_budget_panel = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_ammunition_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_small_arms_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_artillery_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_tanks_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_aeroplanes_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_manowars_budget_panel
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_ironclads_budget_panel
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

#grain

grain_buy_on = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_grain_var
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
grain_sell_off = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_grain_var
			value = 0
		}

	}
}
grain_buy_on_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_grain_var = 1
	}
}
grain_sell_off_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_grain_var = 0
	}
}

#grain
increase_grain_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		grain_market_panel_quantity <= 1000000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_market_panel_quantity
				var:grain_market_panel_quantity < 1000000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_market_panel_quantity
				add = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		grain_market_panel_quantity > 50000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_market_panel_quantity
				var:grain_market_panel_quantity > 50000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_market_panel_quantity
				subtract = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_shown = {
		lead_market_panel_quantity > 50000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lead_market_panel_quantity
				var:lead_market_panel_quantity > 50000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = lead_market_panel_quantity
				subtract = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		gold_reserves > international_buy_grain_budget_panel
		stockpiling_grain_var_state < 9000000
		has_technology_researched = international_trade
	}
}

#grain
buy_grain_budget_panel = {
	effect = {
		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = international_buy_grain_budget_panel
			#add = international_buy_grain_budget_panel
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_grain_state_1
					add = owner.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = international_buy_oil_budget_panel
			#add = international_buy_oil_budget_panel
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_oil_state_1
					add = owner.var:oil_market_panel_quantity
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

sell_limit_var_show = {
	is_shown = {
		var:sell_limit_var_1 > 0
	}
}

sell_limit_var_show_0 = {
	is_shown = {
		var:sell_limit_var_1 = 0
	}
}

#grain_in_curency
buy_grain_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = grain_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = scope:target.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.grain_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_grain_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_grain_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = grain_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = scope:target.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.grain_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_grain_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		player.stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		stockpiling_money_state > buy_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

		player.var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#grain_in_gold
buy_grain_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain in gold by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = grain_price
					multiply = money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = scope:target.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = scope:target.var:grain_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_grain_in_gold_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_grain_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.grain_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = scope:target.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price
				value = scope:target.var:grain_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_in_gold_grain_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_grain_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#coal_in_curency
buy_coal_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price
				value = coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = coal_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_1
				value  = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price
				value = scope:target.coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.coal_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = coal_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_coal_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_coal_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

buy_coal_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_coal_var_state > player.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_coal_market_panel
		player.var:coal_contract_1_year = 0
		var:coal_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_coal_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_coal_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		player.stockpiling_coal_var_state > player.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
		stockpiling_money_state > buy_coal_market_panel
		player.var:coal_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

		player.var:coal_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_coal_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#coal_in_gold
buy_coal_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price
				value = coal_price
			}

			#coal in gold by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = coal_price
					multiply = money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_1
				value  = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price
				value = scope:target.coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = scope:target.var:coal_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = coal_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_coal_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_coal_in_gold_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_coal_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}

			}

				value = coal_price
			}

				name = coal_buy_price_by_price_in_gold

					add = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.coal_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_1
				value  = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}

				name = sulfur_buy_price
				value = scope:target.sulfur_price
			}

			#sulfur price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = scope:target.var:sulfur_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_sulfur_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_sulfur_in_gold_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_sulfur_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#sulfur quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:sulfur_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#sulfur price
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_buy_price
				value = sulfur_price
			}

			#sulfur price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:sulfur_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.sulfur_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#sulfur quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_sell_1
				value  = var:sulfur_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#sulfur price
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_sell_price
				value = scope:target.sulfur_price
			}

			#sulfur price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_sell_price_by_price
				value = scope:target.var:sulfur_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = sulfur_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_sulfur_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_in_gold_sulfur_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_sulfur_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_sulfur_var_state > player.var:sulfur_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_sulfur_market_panel
		player.var:sulfur_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sulfur_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_sulfur_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_sulfur_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		player.stockpiling_sulfur_var_state > player.var:sulfur_market_panel_quantity
		stockpiling_money_state > buy_sulfur_market_panel
		player.var:sulfur_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

		player.var:sulfur_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_sulfur_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#lead_in_curency
buy_lead_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#lead quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:lead_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#lead price
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_sell_price
				value = lead_price
			}

			#lead price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:lead_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = lead_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#lead quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_buy_1
				value  = var:lead_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#lead price
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_buy_price
				value = scope:target.lead_price
			}

			#lead price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = lead_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:lead_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.lead_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = lead_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_lead_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_lead_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price
				value = dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = dye_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_1
				value  = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price
				value = scope:target.dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.dye_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = dye_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_dye_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_dye_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_dye_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_dye_var_state > player.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_dye_market_panel
		player.var:dye_contract_1_year = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}

		custom_tooltip = {

		}

		player.var:dye_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

#dye_in_gold
buy_dye_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price
				value = dye_price
			}

			#dye in gold by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = dye_price
					multiply = money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_1
				value  = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price
				value = scope:target.dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = scope:target.var:dye_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = dye_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_dye_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_dye_in_gold_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_dye_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price
				value = dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.dye_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_1
				value  = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price
				value = scope:target.dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price_by_price
				value = scope:target.var:dye_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = dye_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_dye_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_in_gold_dye_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			#rubber price
			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_buy_price
				value = rubber_price
			}

			#rubber price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:rubber_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.rubber_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#rubber quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_sell_1
				value  = var:rubber_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#rubber price
			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_sell_price
				value = scope:target.rubber_price
			}

			#rubber price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_sell_price_by_price
				value = scope:target.var:rubber_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = rubber_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_rubber_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_in_gold_rubber_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_rubber_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_rubber_var_state > player.var:rubber_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_rubber_market_panel
		player.var:rubber_contract_1_year = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_rubber_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_rubber_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {

		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}

		stockpiling_money_state > buy_rubber_market_panel
		player.var:rubber_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

		player.var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_rubber_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#ammunition_in_curency
buy_ammunition_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price
				value = ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = ammunition_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_1
				value  = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price
				value = scope:target.ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.ammunition_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_ammunition_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_ammunition_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#artillery quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#artillery price
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_price
				value = artillery_price
			}

			#artillery price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = artillery_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#artillery quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_1
				value  = var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#artillery price
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_price
				value = scope:target.artillery_price
			}

			#artillery price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.artillery_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_artillery_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_artillery_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

#artillery_in_gold
buy_artillery_market_in_gold_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#artillery quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#artillery price
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_price
				value = artillery_price
			}

			#artillery in gold by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = artillery_price
					multiply = money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#artillery quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_1
				value  = var:artillery_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#artillery price
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_price
				value = scope:target.artillery_price
			}

			#artillery price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = scope:target.var:artillery_sell_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = artillery_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_artillery_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_artillery_in_gold_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#aeroplanes quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_buy_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:aeroplanes_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#aeroplanes price
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_buy_price
				value = aeroplanes_price
			}

			#aeroplanes price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:aeroplanes_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.aeroplanes_price
					multiply = scope:player_country.money_value_rapported_inflation
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#aeroplanes quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_sell_1
				value  = var:aeroplanes_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#aeroplanes price
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_sell_price
				value = scope:target.aeroplanes_price
			}

			#aeroplanes price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_sell_price_by_price
				value = scope:target.var:aeroplanes_buy_price_by_price_in_gold
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_aeroplanes_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_in_gold_aeroplanes_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_aeroplanes_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state > player.var:aeroplanes_market_panel_quantity
		player.stockpiling_money_state > buy_aeroplanes_market_panel
		player.var:aeroplanes_contract_1_year = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_aeroplanes_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_aeroplanes_market_panel_in_gold_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		player.stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state > player.var:aeroplanes_market_panel_quantity
		stockpiling_money_state > buy_aeroplanes_market_panel
		player.var:aeroplanes_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0

		player.var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_aeroplanes_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#manowars_in_curency
buy_manowars_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country
			
		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#manowars quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_sell_1 
				value  = scope:player_country.var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#manowars price
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_sell_price
				value = manowars_price
			}

			#manowars price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = manowars_price
				}
			}
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#manowars quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_buy_1
				value  = var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#manowars price
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_buy_price
				value = scope:target.manowars_price
			}

			#manowars price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.manowars_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = manowars_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_manowars_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_manowars_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

#money
money_buy_on = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_money_var
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
money_sell_on = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_money_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
money_buy_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_money_var = 1
	}
}
money_sell_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_money_var = 0
	}
}

#grain

#quatituy
increase_grain_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_quantity
		#var:grain_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_quantity
				#var:grain_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_quantity
		var:grain_store_quantity > 1000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_quantity
				var:grain_store_quantity > 1000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_grain_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_quantity
		grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_quantity
				grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_quantity
		var:grain_release_quantity > 1000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_quantity
				var:grain_release_quantity > 1000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#time
increase_grain_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_month
		var:grain_store_month < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_month
		var:grain_store_month > 12
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_month
				var:grain_store_month > 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_grain_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_month
		grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_month
		var:grain_release_month > 12
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_month
				var:grain_release_month > 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_grain_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_grain_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_release_status = 1
	}

set_grain_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_grain_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_grain_var_1 < 10000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_grain_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_grain_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_grain_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_grain_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_grain_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state

		grain_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_grain_var_state
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = grain_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity_1_year
			value = grain_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_grain_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_grain_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_wood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_store_quantity
		#var:wood_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_store_quantity
				#var:wood_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_wood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_store_quantity
		var:wood_store_quantity > 1000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_store_quantity
				var:wood_store_quantity > 1000
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_wood_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_release_quantity
		wood_release_predicted < stockpiling_wood_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_release_quantity
				wood_release_predicted < stockpiling_wood_var_state
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_release_quantity

		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0

				has_variable = wood_release_quantity

				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

default_wood = {
	is_shown = {
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_wood_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:wood_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_wood_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:wood_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_wood_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_wood_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_wood_1
				remove_modifier = store_wood_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_wood_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_wood_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_wood_var_1 < 10000000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
		var:wood_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_wood = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_wood_var_1
			value = wood_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month_fixe
			value = var:wood_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_wood_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_wood_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_wood_1
				remove_modifier = store_wood_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_wood_1
					multiplier = wood_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_coal_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#coal_release_predicted < stockpiling_coal_var_state

		coal_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_coal_var_state
		var:coal_store_status = 0
		var:coal_release_status = 0
		var:coal_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_coal = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_coal_var_1
			value = coal_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_month_fixe
			value = var:coal_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_quantity_1_year
			value = coal_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_coal_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_coal_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_coal_1
				remove_modifier = release_coal_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_coal_1
					multiplier = coal_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_coal_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#iron

#quatituy
increase_iron_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_store_quantity
		#var:iron_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_store_quantity
				#var:iron_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:iron_store_status = 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_iron_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_store_quantity
		var:iron_store_quantity > 1000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_store_quantity
				var:iron_store_quantity > 1000
				var:iron_store_status = 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_iron_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_release_quantity
		iron_release_predicted < stockpiling_iron_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_release_quantity
				iron_release_predicted < stockpiling_iron_var_state
				var:iron_store_status = 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_iron_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_release_quantity
		var:iron_release_quantity > 1000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_release_quantity
				var:iron_release_quantity > 1000
				var:iron_store_status = 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#time
increase_iron_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_store_month
		var:iron_store_month < 1000000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_iron_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_store_month
		var:iron_store_month > 12
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_store_month
				var:iron_store_month > 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_iron_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_release_month
		iron_release_predicted < stockpiling_iron_var_state
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_iron_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_release_month
		var:iron_release_month > 12
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_release_month
				var:iron_release_month > 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

default_iron = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_iron_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_iron_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_iron_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_iron_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_iron_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_iron_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_iron_var_1 < 10000000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
		var:iron_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_iron = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_iron_var_1
			value = iron_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month_fixe
			value = var:iron_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_iron_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_iron_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_iron_1
					multiplier = iron_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_iron_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_iron_var_1
			value = iron_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {

				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_iron_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_iron_1
					multiplier = iron_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			value = var:sulfur_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = sulfur_release_quantity_1_year
			value = sulfur_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_sulfur_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_sulfur_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_sulfur_1
				remove_modifier = release_sulfur_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_sulfur_1
					multiplier = sulfur_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = sulfur_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = sulfur_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_sulfur_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_lead_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = lead_store_quantity
		#var:lead_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lead_store_quantity
				#var:lead_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:lead_store_status = 0
				var:lead_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = lead_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_lead_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = lead_store_quantity
		var:lead_store_quantity > 1000
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lead_store_quantity
				var:lead_store_quantity > 1000
				var:lead_store_status = 0
				var:lead_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = lead_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

		has_variable = lead_release_quantity
		lead_release_predicted < stockpiling_lead_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod

default_lead = {
	is_shown = {
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_lead_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:lead_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_lead_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:lead_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_lead_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_lead_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_lead_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_lead_var_1 < 10000000
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_lead_var_1
			value = lead_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_lead_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_lead_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_lead_1
					multiplier = lead_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_lead_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_lead_var_1
			value = lead_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {

				has_building = building_national_stockpile

			}

				building_type = building_national_stockpile

		}

			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_lead_1
					multiplier = lead_store_for_modifier
				}
			}

	}

set_release_lead_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#lead_release_predicted < stockpiling_lead_var_state

		lead_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_lead_var_state
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = lead_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity_1_year
			value = lead_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_lead_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_lead_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_lead_1
					multiplier = lead_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

			name = oil_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_oil_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_dye_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = dye_store_quantity
		#var:dye_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dye_store_quantity
				#var:dye_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:dye_store_status = 0
				var:dye_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dye_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_dye_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = dye_store_quantity
		var:dye_store_quantity > 1000
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {

			limit = {
				has_variable = dye_store_quantity

				var:dye_store_status = 0
				var:dye_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dye_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}

#####################################################################################################################################################

default_dye = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_dye_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_dye_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_dye_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_dye_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_dye_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_dye_var_1 < 10000000
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
		var:dye_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_dye = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_dye_var_1
			value = dye_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_dye_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_dye_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_dye_1
					multiplier = dye_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_dye_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_dye_var_1
			value = dye_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_dye_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_dye_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_dye_1
					multiplier = dye_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_dye_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#dye_release_predicted < stockpiling_dye_var_state

		dye_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_dye_var_state
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
		var:dye_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_dye = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_var_1
			value = dye_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity_1_year
			value = dye_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_dye_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_dye_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_dye_1
					multiplier = dye_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#quatituy
increase_rubber_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_store_quantity
		#var:rubber_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_store_quantity
				#var:rubber_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:rubber_store_status = 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_rubber_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_store_quantity
		var:rubber_store_quantity > 1000
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_store_quantity
				var:rubber_store_quantity > 1000
				var:rubber_store_status = 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_rubber_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_release_quantity
		rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_release_quantity
				rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state
				var:rubber_store_status = 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_rubber_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_release_quantity
		var:rubber_release_quantity > 1000
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_release_quantity
				var:rubber_release_quantity > 1000
				var:rubber_store_status = 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#time
increase_rubber_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_store_month
		var:rubber_store_month < 1000000
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_rubber_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_store_month
		var:rubber_store_month > 12
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_store_month
				var:rubber_store_month > 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_rubber_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_release_month
		rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_rubber_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = rubber_release_month
		var:rubber_release_month > 12
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = rubber_release_month
				var:rubber_release_month > 0
				var:rubber_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = rubber_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

default_rubber = {
	is_shown = {
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_rubber_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:rubber_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_rubber_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:rubber_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_rubber_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_rubber_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_rubber_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_rubber_var_1 < 10000000
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
		var:rubber_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_rubber = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_rubber_var_1
			value = rubber_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_month_fixe
			value = var:rubber_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_rubber_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_rubber_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_rubber_1
					multiplier = rubber_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_rubber_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_rubber_var_1
			value = rubber_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_rubber_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_rubber_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_rubber_1
					multiplier = rubber_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_rubber_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state

		rubber_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_rubber_var_state
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_rubber = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_var_1
			value = rubber_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_month_fixe
			value = var:rubber_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity_1_year
			value = rubber_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_rubber_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_rubber_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_rubber_1
					multiplier = rubber_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#quatituy
increase_small_arms_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
		#var:small_arms_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
				#var:small_arms_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:small_arms_store_status = 0
				var:small_arms_release_status = 0
