default_small_arms = {
	is_shown = {
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_small_arms_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:small_arms_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_small_arms_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:small_arms_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_small_arms_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_small_arms_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_small_arms_1
				remove_modifier = store_small_arms_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_small_arms_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_small_arms_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_small_arms_var_1 < 10000000
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
		var:small_arms_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_small_arms = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_small_arms_var_1
			value = small_arms_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_month_fixe
			value = var:small_arms_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_small_arms_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_small_arms_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_small_arms_1
				remove_modifier = store_small_arms_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_small_arms_1
					multiplier = small_arms_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_small_arms_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_small_arms_var_1
			value = small_arms_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_small_arms_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_small_arms_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_small_arms_1
				remove_modifier = store_small_arms_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_small_arms_1
					multiplier = small_arms_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_small_arms_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#small_arms_release_predicted < stockpiling_small_arms_var_state

		small_arms_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_small_arms_var_state
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_small_arms = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_small_arms_var_1
			value = small_arms_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_month_fixe
			value = var:small_arms_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_quantity_1_year
			value = small_arms_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_small_arms_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_small_arms_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_small_arms_1
				remove_modifier = release_small_arms_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_small_arms_1
					multiplier = small_arms_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_small_arms_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_tanks_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = tanks_store_quantity
		#var:tanks_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = tanks_store_quantity
				#var:tanks_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:tanks_store_status = 0
				var:tanks_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = tanks_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_tanks_quantity_store = {

		has_variable = tanks_store_quantity
		var:tanks_store_quantity > 1000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0

default_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_tanks_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_tanks_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_tanks_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_tanks_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_tanks_1
				remove_modifier = store_tanks_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_tanks_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_tanks_var_1 < 10000000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
		var:tanks_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month_fixe
			value = var:tanks_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_tanks_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_tanks_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_tanks_1
				remove_modifier = store_tanks_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_tanks_1
					multiplier = tanks_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_tanks_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_tanks_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_tanks_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_tanks_1
				remove_modifier = store_tanks_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_tanks_1
					multiplier = tanks_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_tanks_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#tanks_release_predicted < stockpiling_tanks_var_state

		tanks_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_tanks_var_state
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_month_fixe
			value = var:tanks_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity_1_year
			value = tanks_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_tanks_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_tanks_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_tanks_1
				remove_modifier = release_tanks_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_tanks_1
					multiplier = tanks_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#manowars

#quatituy
increase_manowars_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_store_quantity
		#var:manowars_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_store_quantity
				#var:manowars_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:manowars_store_status = 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_manowars_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_store_quantity
		var:manowars_store_quantity > 1000
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_store_quantity
				var:manowars_store_quantity > 1000
				var:manowars_store_status = 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_manowars_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_release_quantity
		manowars_release_predicted < stockpiling_manowars_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_release_quantity
				manowars_release_predicted < stockpiling_manowars_var_state
				var:manowars_store_status = 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_manowars_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_release_quantity
		var:manowars_release_quantity > 1000
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_release_quantity
				var:manowars_release_quantity > 1000
				var:manowars_store_status = 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#time
increase_manowars_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_store_month
		var:manowars_store_month < 1000000
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_manowars_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_store_month
		var:manowars_store_month > 12
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_store_month
				var:manowars_store_month > 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_manowars_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_release_month
		manowars_release_predicted < stockpiling_manowars_var_state
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_manowars_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = manowars_release_month
		var:manowars_release_month > 12
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manowars_release_month
				var:manowars_release_month > 0
				var:manowars_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manowars_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

default_manowars = {
	is_shown = {
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_manowars_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:manowars_store_status = 1
	}
}

release_manowars_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:manowars_release_status = 1
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################

set_manowars_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_manowars_0
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_manowars_1
				remove_modifier = store_manowars_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_manowars_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

set_store_manowars_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_manowars_var_1 < 10000000
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
		var:manowars_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_manowars = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_manowars_var_1
			value = manowars_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_month_fixe
			value = var:manowars_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_manowars_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_manowars_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_manowars_1
				remove_modifier = store_manowars_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_manowars_1
					multiplier = manowars_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_manowars_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_manowars_var_1
			value = manowars_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_manowars_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_store_manowars_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_manowars_1
				remove_modifier = store_manowars_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_manowars_1
					multiplier = manowars_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_manowars_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#manowars_release_predicted < stockpiling_manowars_var_state

		manowars_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_manowars_var_state
		var:manowars_store_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0
		var:manowars_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_manowars = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_manowars_var_1
			value = manowars_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_month_fixe
			value = var:manowars_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_release_quantity_1_year
			value = manowars_release_predicted
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_manowars_0
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_national_stockpile
				production_method = pm_release_manowars_1
			}
		}
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_manowars_1
				remove_modifier = release_manowars_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_manowars_1
					multiplier = manowars_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manowars_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_manowars_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

				add = 500

				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_ironclads_1
				remove_modifier = release_ironclads_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_ironclads_1
					multiplier = ironclads_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ironclads_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
